  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'MistFiner_BWalk'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'MistFiner_Cancel_D'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'MistFiner_Cancel_E'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'MistFiner_FWalk'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'MistFiner_FDash'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'MistFiner_BDash'

    whiffCancelOptionBufferTime: s32'MistFiner_Cancel_D', 3
    whiffCancelOptionBufferTime: s32'MistFiner_Cancel_E', 3
    whiffCancelOptionBufferTime: s32'MistFiner_FDash', 3
    whiffCancelOptionBufferTime: s32'MistFiner_BDash', 3
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'AirMistFiner_Stance'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'AirMistFiner_Cancel_D'
    addWhiffCancelOption: s32'AirMistFiner_Cancel_E'

    whiffCancelOptionBufferTime: s32'AirMistFiner_BDash', 3
  endIf: 
  upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
      checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_P)
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        addWhiffCancelOption: s32'MistFiner_Attack_A'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(2)
      checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_K)
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        addWhiffCancelOption: s32'MistFiner_Attack_B'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(3)
      checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_S)
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        addWhiffCancelOption: s32'MistFiner_Attack_C'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(11)
      checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_P)
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        addWhiffCancelOption: s32'AirMistFiner_Attack_A'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(12)
      checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_K)
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        addWhiffCancelOption: s32'AirMistFiner_Attack_B'
      endIf: 
    endIf:

      checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_S)
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        addWhiffCancelOption: s32'AirMistFiner_Attack_C'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:
